### All languages

[google / python-fire](../../../../../google/python-fire)  
Python Fire is a library for automatically generating command line interfaces (CLIs) from absolutely any Python object.  

[forter / security-101-for-saas-startups](../../../../../forter/security-101-for-saas-startups)  
security tips for startups  

[freeCodeCamp / freeCodeCamp](../../../../../freeCodeCamp/freeCodeCamp)  
The https://freeCodeCamp.com open source codebase and curriculum. Learn to code and help nonprofits.  

[amaneureka / AtomOS](../../../../../amaneureka/AtomOS)  
A Multitasking Monolithic Kernel based x86 targetting Operating System written in C# from scratch aiming for high level implementation of drivers in managed environment and security.  

[alibaba / vlayout](../../../../../alibaba/vlayout)  
Project vlayout is a powerfull LayoutManager extension for RecyclerView, it provides a group of layouts for RecyclerView. Make it able to handle a complicate situation when grid, list and other layouts in the same recyclerview.  

[skyline75489 / what-happens-when-zh_CN](../../../../../skyline75489/what-happens-when-zh_CN)  
What-happens-when 的中文翻译，原仓库 https://github.com/alex/what-happens-when  

[verekia / js-stack-from-scratch](../../../../../verekia/js-stack-from-scratch)  
Step-by-step tutorial to build a modern JavaScript stack from scratch.  

[Pixplicity / HtmlCompat](../../../../../Pixplicity/HtmlCompat)  
Compatibility library for Android's Html class.  

[lhartikk / naivechain](../../../../../lhartikk/naivechain)  
A blockchain implementation in 200 lines of code  

[cs01 / gdbgui](../../../../../cs01/gdbgui)  
A modern, browser-based frontend to gdb (gnu debugger). Add breakpoints, view stack traces, and more in C, C++, Go, and Rust! Simply run gdbgui from the terminal and a new tab will open in your browser.  

[gchaincl / httplab](../../../../../gchaincl/httplab)  
An interactive web server  

[lin-xin / manage-system](../../../../../lin-xin/manage-system)  
基于Vue.js 2.x系列 + Element UI 后台管理系统解决方案  

[unsplash / react-trend](../../../../../unsplash/react-trend)  
📈 Simple, elegant spark lines  

[marcobambini / gravity](../../../../../marcobambini/gravity)  
Gravity Programming Language  

[JulianGaal / python-cheat-sheet](../../../../../JulianGaal/python-cheat-sheet)  
Python for Data Science - NumPy, Pandas, SciKit Learn ...  

[mattallty / Caporal.js](../../../../../mattallty/Caporal.js)  
A full-featured framework for building command line applications (cli) with node.js  

[BafS / Gutenberg](../../../../../BafS/Gutenberg)  
Modern framework to print the web correctly.  

[robertlevonyan / materialChipView](../../../../../robertlevonyan/materialChipView)  
Material Chip view. Can be used as tags for categories, contacts or creating text clouds  

[thomasj02 / DeepLearningProjectWorkflow](../../../../../thomasj02/DeepLearningProjectWorkflow)  
Machine Learning Workflow, from Andrew Ng's lecture at Deep Learning Summer School 2016  

[marcuswestin / store.js](../../../../../marcuswestin/store.js)  
Cross-browser storage for all use cases • Used across the web • See below for v2.0 news!  

[kamranahmedse / design-patterns-for-humans](../../../../../kamranahmedse/design-patterns-for-humans)  
Design Patterns for Humans™ - An ultra-simplified explanation  

[NotThePolice / sqlmap-crawler](../../../../../NotThePolice/sqlmap-crawler)

[cforler / Ada-Crypto-Library](../../../../../cforler/Ada-Crypto-Library)  
The libadacrypt-dev is a crypto library for Ada with a nice API. It is written for the i386 and x86_64 hardware architecture and supports AES, Twofish, 3DES, Serpent SHA-1/256/384/512, DSA, OAEP-RSA, HMAC, CMAC, SIV, OCB, Nonces, Elliptic Curves. etc. It also contains regression tests consisting of over 400 tests. Dependencies: make and gnat-4.9.

[frkunz / stELMOD](../../../../../frkunz/stELMOD)  
stELMOD is a stochastic optimization model to analyze the impact of uncertain wind generation on the dayahead and intraday electricity markets as well as network congestion management. The consecutive clearing of the electricity markets is incorporated by a rolling planning procedure resembling the market process of most European markets.
